        function adjustViewport() {
            var screenWidthPx = Math.min($(window).width(), window.screen.width);
            var siteWidthPx = 1100; // min width of site
            var ratio = Math.min(screenWidthPx / siteWidthPx, 1.0);
            var viewport = "width=device-width, initial-scale=" + ratio;
            $('#viewport').attr('content', viewport);
            var style = $('<style>html * { max-height: 1000000px; }</style>');
            $('html > head').append(style);
        }

        if ( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
            adjustViewport();
        }

<script type="text/javascript">
    var queryMobile = Codeforces.queryString.mobile;
    if (queryMobile === "true" || queryMobile === "false") {
        Codeforces.putToStorage("useMobile", queryMobile == "true");
    } else {
        var useMobile = Codeforces.getFromStorage("useMobile");
        if (useMobile === true || useMobile === false) {
            if (useMobile != false) {
                Codeforces.redirect(Codeforces.updateUrlParameter(document.location.href, "mobile", useMobile));
            }
        }
    }
</script>

        $(document).ready(function () {
    (function () {
        jQuery.expr[':'].containsCI = function(elem, index, match) {
            return !match || !match.length || match.length < 4 || !match[3] || (
                    elem.textContent || elem.innerText || jQuery(elem).text() || ''
            ).toLowerCase().indexOf(match[3].toLowerCase()) >= 0;
        }
    }(jQuery));

    $.ajaxPrefilter(function(options, originalOptions, xhr) {
        var csrf = Codeforces.getCsrfToken();

        if (csrf) {
            var data = originalOptions.data;
            if (originalOptions.data !== undefined) {
                if (Object.prototype.toString.call(originalOptions.data) === '[object String]') {
                    data = $.deparam(originalOptions.data);
                }
            } else {
                data = {};
            }
            options.data = $.param($.extend(data, { csrf_token: csrf }));
        }
    });

    window.getCodeforcesServerTime = function(callback) {
        $.post("/data/time", {}, callback, "json");
    }

    window.updateTypography = function () {
        $("div.ttypography code").addClass("tt");
        $("div.ttypography pre>code").addClass("prettyprint").removeClass("tt");
        $("div.ttypography table").addClass("bordertable");
        prettyPrint();
    }

    $.ajaxSetup({ scriptCharset: "utf-8" ,contentType: "application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8", headers: {
        'X-Csrf-Token': Codeforces.getCsrfToken()
    }});

    function showAnnouncements(json) {
        //info("j=" + JSON.stringify(json));

        if (json.t != "a") {
            return;
        }
        // console.log("Got announcement from channel");
        setTimeout(function() {
            Codeforces.showAnnouncements(json.d, "en");
        }, Math.random() * 500);
    }
    if (Codeforces.getParticipantChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getParticipantChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    if (Codeforces.getContestChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getContestChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    if (Codeforces.getGlobalChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getGlobalChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    if (Codeforces.getUserChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getUserChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    $(".clickable-title").click(function() {
        Codeforces.alert($(this).attr("title"));
    }).css("position", "relative").css("bottom", "3px");


    Codeforces.reformatTimes();
    Codeforces.initializePubSub();

    Codeforces.setupSpoilers();
    Codeforces.setupTutorials("/data/problemTutorial");
        });

$(document).ready(function () {

        var voteValue = $(this).attr("voteValue");
        $("#vote-value-filterDifficultyLowerBorder").val(voteValue);
        $("#vote-current-filterDifficultyLowerBorder").css("width", voteValue * 25 + "px");

        $("#vote-value-filterDifficultyLowerBorder").val("0");

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("select[name=filterContestType]").change(function () {
            if ($(this).val() === "Official ACM-ICPC Contest") {
                $("div.icpc-region").show();
            } else {
                $("div.icpc-region").hide();
                $("select[name=filterIcpcRegion]").val("");
            }
        });

        $("select[name=order]").change(function () {
            if ($(this).val() === "") {
                $("div.additional-order").hide();
                $("select[name=additionalOrder]").val("");
            } else {
                $("div.additional-order").show();
            }
        });

        $("#gym-filter-form").submit(function () {
            var form = $("#gym-filter-form");

            form.find("select[value=]").remove();

            form.find("input[name=filterDurationLowerBorder],"
                    + "input[name=filterDurationUpperBorder],"
                    + "input[name=filterDifficultyLowerBorder],"
                    + "input[name=filterDifficultyUpperBorder],"
                    + "input[name=filterRatingLowerBorder],"
                    + "input[name=filterRatingUpperBorder]").each(function () {
                        var e = $(this);
                        if (e.val() === "" || e.val() === "0") {
                            e.remove();
                        }
                    }
            );
        });
    });
</script>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(".searchButton").click(function () {
            $.closest("form#searchContestForm").submit();
            return false;
        });

        var getContests = function(callbackFunc) {
            var queryInput = $("input[name=problemQuery]");
            var query = queryInput.attr("value");

            $.post("/gyms",
                    { action: "findContests", searchQuery: query},
                    function(response) {
                        var result = response["success"] === "true";
                        callbackFunc(result)
                    },
                    "json"
            );
        };

        $("form#searchContestForm").submit(function () {
            getContests(function(result) {});
            return false;
        });

        $("input[name=searchQuery]").autocomplete("/data/gym/suggest/contest?showMashups=false", {
            delay: 200,
            width: 250,
            selectFirst: false,
            matchContains: true,
            minChars: 1,
            max: 150
        });
    });
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
                // Create new ':containsIgnoreCase' selector for search
                jQuery.expr[':'].containsIgnoreCase = function(a, i, m) {
                    return jQuery(a).text().toUpperCase()
                            .indexOf(m[3].toUpperCase()) >= 0;
                };

                if (window.updateDatatableFilter == undefined) {
                    window.updateDatatableFilter = function(i) {
                        var parent = $(i).parent().parent().parent().parent();
                        $("tr.no-items", parent).remove();
                        $("tr", parent).hide().removeClass('visible');
                        var text = $(i).val();
                        if (text) {
                            $("tr" + ":containsIgnoreCase('" + text + "')", parent).show().addClass('visible');
                        } else {
                            parent.find(".rowCount").text("");
                            $("tr", parent).show().addClass('visible');
                        }

                        var found = false;
                        var visibleRowCount = 0;
                        $("tr", parent).each(function () {
                            if (!found) {
                                if ($(this).find("th").size() > 0) {
                                    $(this).show().addClass('visible');
                                    found = true;
                                }
                            }
                            if ($(this).hasClass('visible')) {
                                visibleRowCount++;
                            }
                        });
                        if (text) {
                            parent.find(".rowCount").text("Matches: " + (visibleRowCount - (found ? 1 : 0)));
                        }
                        if (visibleRowCount == (found ? 1 : 0)) {
                            $("<tr class='no-items visible'><td style=\"text-align:left;\"colspan=\"32\">No items<\/td><\/tr>").appendTo($(parent).find('table'));
                        }
                        $(parent).find("tr td").removeClass("dark");
                        $(parent).find("tr.visible:odd td").addClass("dark");
                    }

                    $(".datatable .closed").click(function () {
                        var parent = $(this).parent();
                        $(this).hide();
                        $(".filter", parent).fadeIn(function () {
                            $("input", parent).val("").focus().css("border", "1px solid #aaa");
                        });
                    });

                    $(".datatable .opened").click(function () {
                        var parent = $(this).parent().parent();
                        $(".filter", parent).fadeOut(function () {
                            $(".closed", parent).show();
                            $("input", parent).val("").each(function () {
                                window.updateDatatableFilter(this);
                            });
                        });
                    });

                    $(".datatable .filter input").keyup(function(e) {
                        window.updateDatatableFilter(this);
                        e.preventDefault();
                        e.stopPropagation();
                    });

                    $(".datatable table").each(function () {
                        var found = false;
                        $("tr", this).each(function () {
                            if (!found && $(this).find("th").size() == 0) {
                                found = true;
                            }
                        });
                        if (!found) {
                            $("<tr class='no-items visible'><td style=\"text-align:left;\"colspan=\"32\">No items<\/td><\/tr>").appendTo(this);
                        }
                    });

                    // Applies styles to datatables.
                    $(".datatable").each(function () {
                        $(this).find("tr:first th").addClass("top");
                        $(this).find("tr:last td").addClass("bottom");
                        $(this).find("tr:odd td").addClass("dark");
                        $(this).find("tr td:first-child, tr th:first-child").addClass("left");
                        $(this).find("tr td:last-child, tr th:last-child").addClass("right");
                    });

                    $(".datatable table.tablesorter").each(function () {
                        $(this).bind("sortEnd", function () {
                            $(".datatable").each(function () {
                                $(this).find("th, td")
                                    .removeClass("top").removeClass("bottom")
                                    .removeClass("left").removeClass("right")
                                    .removeClass("dark");
                                $(this).find("tr:first th").addClass("top");
                                $(this).find("tr:last td").addClass("bottom");
                                $(this).find("tr:odd td").addClass("dark");
                                $(this).find("tr td:first-child, tr th:first-child").addClass("left");
                                $(this).find("tr td:last-child, tr th:last-child").addClass("right");
                            });
                        });
                    });
                }
        });
    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
if (!window.hasContestDescriptionLinkHandler) {
    window.hasContestDescriptionLinkHandler = true;
    $(".contest-description-link").click(function () {
        var contestId = $(this).attr("data-contestId");
        $.post("/data/contestInfo", {action: "getDescription", contestId: contestId}, function(result) {
            if (result["success"] == "true")
                Codeforces.alert(result["description"]);
        }, "json");
        return false;
    });
}

$(".toggle-mashup-manager").click(function () {
    $(this).attr("disabled", "disabled");
    var contestId = $(this).attr("data-contestId");
    var newValue = $(this).is(":checked");
    $.post("/data/mashup",
        {contestId: contestId, action: "toggleMashupContestManagerMode", newValue: newValue},
        function(response) {
            if (response["success"] === "true") {
                Codeforces.reload();
            } else {
                Codeforces.showMessage("Unable to toggle mashup contest manager mode");
                $(this).removeAttr("disabled");
            }
        },
        "json"
    );
    return false;
});
        });
    </script>
</div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
        $.post("/data/contests", {action: "getSolvedProblemCountsByContest"}, function(response) {
        var c = response["solvedProblemCountsByContestId"];
        var p = response["problemCountsByContestId"];
        $(".contests-table tr[data-contestId]").each(function () {
        var contestId = $(this).attr("data-contestId");
        var problemCount = c[contestId];
        var totalCount = p[contestId];
        if (problemCount && problemCount > 0) {
        var td = $(this).find("td.state");
        if (problemCount < totalCount)
        td.css("background-color", "#def");
        else
        td.css("background-color", "#D4EDC9");
        td.append("<div class='notice small' style='margin-top: 0.5em;'>Solved: " + problemCount + " out of " + totalCount + "</div>");
        }
        });
        }, "json");
        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
function handlePaginationKeyboardEvent(right) {
    var pageIndex = parseInt($(".pagination").find("span.active").attr("pageIndex"));
    if (right) {
        pageIndex++;
    } else {
        pageIndex--;
    }
    $(".pagination").find("span[pageIndex=" + pageIndex + "]").each(function () {
        Codeforces.redirect($(this).find("a").attr("href"));
    });
}
$(document).keydown(function (e) {
     var code = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
     if (e.ctrlKey) {
        if (code == 37 || code == 39) {
            handlePaginationKeyboardEvent(code == 39);
        }
     }
});
        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
            if ($(window).width() < 1600) {
                $('.button-up').css('width', '30px').css('line-height', '30px').css('font-size', '20px');
            }

            if ($(window).width() >= 1200) {
                $ (window).scroll (function () {
                    if ($ (this).scrollTop () > 100) {
                        $ ('.button-up').fadeIn();
                    } else {
                        $ ('.button-up').fadeOut();
                    }
                });

                $('.button-up').click(function () {
                    $('body,html').animate({
                        scrollTop: 0
                    }, 500);
                    return false;
                });

                $('.button-up').hover(function () {
                    $(this).animate({
                        'opacity':'1'
                    }).css({'background-color':'#e7ebf0','color':'#6a86a4'});
                }, function () {
                    $(this).animate({
                        'opacity':'0.7'
                    }).css({'background':'none','color':'#d3dbe4'});;
                });
            }
            Codeforces.focusOnError();
        });
    </script>

        <script type="application/javascript">
            $(function() {
                $(".userListMarker").click(function() {
                    $.post("/data/lists", {action: "findTouched"}, function(json) {
                        Codeforces.facebox(".userListsFacebox");
                        var tbody = $("#facebox tbody");
                        tbody.empty();
                        for (var i in json) {
                            tbody.append(
                                    $("<tr></tr>").append(
                                            $("<td></td>").attr("data-readKey", json[i].readKey).text(json[i].name)
                                    )
                            );
                        }
                        Codeforces.updateDatatables();
                        tbody.find("td").css("cursor", "pointer").click(function() {
                            document.location = Codeforces.updateUrlParameter(document.location.href, "list", $(this).attr("data-readKey"));
                        });
                    }, "json");
                });
            });
        </script>

    <script type="application/javascript">
        function adjustViewport() {
            var screenWidthPx = Math.min($(window).width(), window.screen.width);
            var siteWidthPx = 1100; // min width of site
            var ratio = Math.min(screenWidthPx / siteWidthPx, 1.0);
            var viewport = "width=device-width, initial-scale=" + ratio;
            $('#viewport').attr('content', viewport);
            var style = $('<style>html * { max-height: 1000000px; }</style>');
            $('html > head').append(style);
        }

        if ( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
            adjustViewport();
        }
    </script>

    var queryMobile = Codeforces.queryString.mobile;
    if (queryMobile === "true" || queryMobile === "false") {
        Codeforces.putToStorage("useMobile", queryMobile == "true");
    } else {
        var useMobile = Codeforces.getFromStorage("useMobile");
        if (useMobile === true || useMobile === false) {
            if (useMobile != false) {
                Codeforces.redirect(Codeforces.updateUrlParameter(document.location.href, "mobile", useMobile));
            }
        }
    }

            return !match || !match.length || match.length < 4 || !match[3] || (
                    elem.textContent || elem.innerText || jQuery(elem).text() || ''
            ).toLowerCase().indexOf(match[3].toLowerCase()) >= 0;

    $.ajaxPrefilter(function(options, originalOptions, xhr) {
        var csrf = Codeforces.getCsrfToken();

        if (csrf) {
            var data = originalOptions.data;
            if (originalOptions.data !== undefined) {
                if (Object.prototype.toString.call(originalOptions.data) === '[object String]') {
                    data = $.deparam(originalOptions.data);
                }
            } else {
                data = {};
            }
            options.data = $.param($.extend(data, { csrf_token: csrf }));
        }
    });

    window.getCodeforcesServerTime = function(callback) {
        $.post("/data/time", {}, callback, "json");
    }

        $("div.ttypography code").addClass("tt");
        $("div.ttypography pre>code").addClass("prettyprint").removeClass("tt");
        $("div.ttypography table").addClass("bordertable");
        prettyPrint();
    }

    function showAnnouncements(json) {
        //info("j=" + JSON.stringify(json));

        if (json.t != "a") {
            return;
        }
        // console.log("Got announcement from channel");
        setTimeout(function() {
            Codeforces.showAnnouncements(json.d, "en");
        }, Math.random() * 500);
    }
    if (Codeforces.getParticipantChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getParticipantChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    if (Codeforces.getContestChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getContestChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    if (Codeforces.getGlobalChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getGlobalChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    if (Codeforces.getUserChannel()) {
        Codeforces.subscribe(Codeforces.getUserChannel(), function(json) {
            showAnnouncements(json);
        });
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
    function updateFriendClickListeners() {
        $("img.removeFriend").click(function () {
            //alert("remove");
            var img = $(this);
            var friendUserId = img.attr("friendUserId");

            $.post("/data/friend", {friendUserId: friendUserId, isAdd: "false"});
            
            var newImg = img.clone().removeClass("removeFriend").addClass("addFriend");
            newImg.attr("src", "http://st.codeforces.com/s/19961/images/icons/star_gray_24.png");
            newImg.attr("title", "Click to add to friends");

            img.css("display", "none");
            img.after(newImg);

            updateFriendClickListeners();
        });

        $("img.addFriend").click(function () {
            //alert("add");
            var img = $(this);
            var friendUserId = img.attr("friendUserId");

            $.post("/data/friend", {friendUserId: friendUserId, isAdd: "true"});

            var newImg = img.clone().removeClass("addFriend").addClass("removeFriend");
            newImg.attr("src", "http://st.codeforces.com/s/19961/images/icons/star_yellow_24.png");
            newImg.attr("title", "Click to remove from friends");

            img.css("display", "none");
            img.after(newImg);

            updateFriendClickListeners();
        });
    }

    updateFriendClickListeners();
        });
    </script>

    { color: '#a00', lineWidth: 1, yaxis: { from: 2900 } },

    { color: '#ffcc88', lineWidth: 1, yaxis: { from: 2200, to: 2299 } },

    { color: '#aaf', lineWidth: 1, yaxis: { from: 1600, to: 1899 } },

    lines: { show: true },
    points: { show: true },
    //xaxis: { tickDecimals: 0, tickSize: 1 },
    xaxis: { mode: "time" },
    yaxis: { min: 1000, max: 2566, ticks: [1200, 1400, 1600, 1900, 2200, 2300, 2400, 2600, 2900] },
    grid: { hoverable: true, markings: markings }
};

var plot = $.plot($("#placeholder"), datas, options);

function showTooltip(x, y, contents) {
    $('<div id="tooltip">' + contents + '</div>').css( {
        position: 'absolute',
        display: 'none',
        top: y - 20,
        left: x + 10,
        border: '1px solid #fdd',
        padding: '2px',
        'font-size' : '11px',
        'background-color': '#fee',
        opacity: 0.80
    }).appendTo("body").fadeIn(200);
}

var ctx = plot.getCanvas().getContext("2d");

var prev = -1;
$("#placeholder").bind("plothover", function (event, pos, item) {
    if (item) {
        if (prev != item.dataIndex) {
            $("#tooltip").remove();
            var params = data[item.seriesIndex][item.dataIndex];

            var total = params[1];
            var change = params[5] > 0 ? "+" + params[5] : params[5];
            var contestName = params[11];
            var contestId = params[2];
            var contestUrl = params[7];
            var rank = params[6];
            var title = params[8];
            var html = "= " + total + " (" + change + "), " + title + "<br/>"
                            + "Rank: " + rank + "<br/>"
                            + "<a href='" + contestUrl + "'>" + contestName + "</a>";
            if (change > 0)
                html += "<br/><a style='font-weight: bold;' href=\"/bestRatingChanges/" + params[10] + "\">Share it!</a>";
            showTooltip(item.pageX, item.pageY, html);
            setTimeout(function () {
                $("#tooltip").fadeOut(200);
                prev = -1;
            }, 4000);
            prev = item.dataIndex;
        }
    }
});

        });

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
            if ($(window).width() < 1600) {
                $('.button-up').css('width', '30px').css('line-height', '30px').css('font-size', '20px');
            }

            if ($(window).width() >= 1200) {
                $ (window).scroll (function () {
                    if ($ (this).scrollTop () > 100) {
                        $ ('.button-up').fadeIn();
                    } else {
                        $ ('.button-up').fadeOut();
                    }
                });

                $('.button-up').click(function () {
                    $('body,html').animate({
                        scrollTop: 0
                    }, 500);
                    return false;
                });

                $('.button-up').hover(function () {
                    $(this).animate({
                        'opacity':'1'
                    }).css({'background-color':'#e7ebf0','color':'#6a86a4'});
                }, function () {
                    $(this).animate({
                        'opacity':'0.7'
                    }).css({'background':'none','color':'#d3dbe4'});;
                });
            }
            Codeforces.focusOnError();
        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
                // Create new ':containsIgnoreCase' selector for search
                jQuery.expr[':'].containsIgnoreCase = function(a, i, m) {
                    return jQuery(a).text().toUpperCase()
                            .indexOf(m[3].toUpperCase()) >= 0;
                };

                if (window.updateDatatableFilter == undefined) {
                    window.updateDatatableFilter = function(i) {
                        var parent = $(i).parent().parent().parent().parent();
                        $("tr.no-items", parent).remove();
                        $("tr", parent).hide().removeClass('visible');
                        var text = $(i).val();
                        if (text) {
                            $("tr" + ":containsIgnoreCase('" + text + "')", parent).show().addClass('visible');
                        } else {
                            parent.find(".rowCount").text("");
                            $("tr", parent).show().addClass('visible');
                        }

                        var found = false;
                        var visibleRowCount = 0;
                        $("tr", parent).each(function () {
                            if (!found) {
                                if ($(this).find("th").size() > 0) {
                                    $(this).show().addClass('visible');
                                    found = true;
                                }
                            }
                            if ($(this).hasClass('visible')) {
                                visibleRowCount++;
                            }
                        });
                        if (text) {
                            parent.find(".rowCount").text("Matches: " + (visibleRowCount - (found ? 1 : 0)));
                        }
                        if (visibleRowCount == (found ? 1 : 0)) {
                            $("<tr class='no-items visible'><td style=\"text-align:left;\"colspan=\"32\">No items<\/td><\/tr>").appendTo($(parent).find('table'));
                        }
                        $(parent).find("tr td").removeClass("dark");
                        $(parent).find("tr.visible:odd td").addClass("dark");
                    }

                    $(".datatable .closed").click(function () {
                        var parent = $(this).parent();
                        $(this).hide();
                        $(".filter", parent).fadeIn(function () {
                            $("input", parent).val("").focus().css("border", "1px solid #aaa");
                        });
                    });

                    $(".datatable .opened").click(function () {
                        var parent = $(this).parent().parent();
                        $(".filter", parent).fadeOut(function () {
                            $(".closed", parent).show();
                            $("input", parent).val("").each(function () {
                                window.updateDatatableFilter(this);
                            });
                        });
                    });

                    $(".datatable .filter input").keyup(function(e) {
                        window.updateDatatableFilter(this);
                        e.preventDefault();
                        e.stopPropagation();
                    });

                    $(".datatable table").each(function () {
                        var found = false;
                        $("tr", this).each(function () {
                            if (!found && $(this).find("th").size() == 0) {
                                found = true;
                            }
                        });
                        if (!found) {
                            $("<tr class='no-items visible'><td style=\"text-align:left;\"colspan=\"32\">No items<\/td><\/tr>").appendTo(this);
                        }
                    });

                    // Applies styles to datatables.
                    $(".datatable").each(function () {
                        $(this).find("tr:first th").addClass("top");
                        $(this).find("tr:last td").addClass("bottom");
                        $(this).find("tr:odd td").addClass("dark");
                        $(this).find("tr td:first-child, tr th:first-child").addClass("left");
                        $(this).find("tr td:last-child, tr th:last-child").addClass("right");
                    });

                    $(".datatable table.tablesorter").each(function () {
